<P style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:4.6pt;margin-bottom:4.6pt;color:#000000'><FONT style=background-color:#FFFFFF><B>Item 3.02 Unregistered Sales of Equity Securities.</B></FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000'><FONT style=background-color:#FFFFFF>On February 9, 2022, Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) closed subscriptions of US$2,701,000.00 in a non-brokered private placement (the &#8220;Private Placement&#8221;) with a small group of investors which included one foreign subscriber. &#160;Proceeds from the&#160;private placement&#160;will be used, in part, to roughly double the Rare Earth Element drill program and for surface work and underground mine development of the Klondike area, lying north of current production from the Skookum shoot. Management believes, once fully completed, that the Klondike will roughly double production from the Golden Chest Mine. </FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000'><FONT style=background-color:#FFFFFF>The Private Placement consisted of shares issued at US$7.50 per common share of restricted common stock.&#160; No warrants were issued in connection with the Private Placement. A total of 6,300 restricted Common Shares were issued pursuant to the Private Placement. </FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000'><FONT style=background-color:#FFFFFF>The above-described sale and issuance of common shares were not registered under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (&#8220;Securities Act&#8221;), or the securities laws of any state, are subject to resale restrictions and may not be offered or sold in the United States absent registration under the Securities Act. The foregoing sale of securities has been determined to be exempt from registration in reliance on Section 4(a)(2) of the Securities Act and the safe harbor provided by Rule 506(b) of Regulation D promulgated thereunder, as transactions by an issuer not involving a public offering, in which the investors are accredited and have acquired the securities for investment purposes only and not with a view to or for sale in connection with any distribution thereof. &nbsp;The Company has also relied on the exclusion from registration provided by Rule 903 of Regulation S under the Securities Act to offer and sell shares to the foreign subscriber.</FONT></P>
<P style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:5pt;margin-bottom:5pt;color:#000000'><FONT style=background-color:#FFFFFF><B>Item 7.01 Regulation FD Disclosure.</B><B> </B></FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000'><FONT style=background-color:#FFFFFF>On February 9, 2022, the Company issued a press release entitled &#8220;Idaho Strategic to Advance Diamond Creek Rare Earth Project, Expands Gold Production into Klondike w/Additional High-Grade Intercepts &#8211;&nbsp;Closes $2.7m Oversubscribed Placement.&#8221; &nbsp;A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. The information in this Current Report on Form 8-K (including the exhibits) is furnished pursuant to Item 7.01 and shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for the purpose of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. &nbsp;This Current Report on Form 8-K will not be deemed an admission as to the materiality of any information in the Report that is required to be disclosed solely by Regulation FD.</FONT></P>

<HEAD>
<TITLE>Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc.</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY>
<DIV style=margin-left:72pt;width:468pt><P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'><FONT style='font-family:Times New Roman'>Exhibit 99.1</FONT></P>
<P align=center style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'><FONT style='font-family:Times New Roman'><IMG src=nrex99z1_1.jpg width=173 height=80 alt='Picture 1' title='Picture 1'></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=center style='font:16pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><B>Idaho Strategic to Advance Diamond Creek Rare Earth Project, Expands Gold Production into Klondike w/Additional High-Grade Intercepts &#8211;&nbsp;Closes $2.7m Oversubscribed Placement</B></P>
<P style='font:16pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>COEUR D'ALENE, Idaho, February 9, 2022 (ACCESSWIRE) &#8211;&nbsp;Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. (OTCQB: NJMC) (&#8220;IDR&#8221;, &#8220;Idaho Strategic&#8221; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) is pleased to announce that its latest high-grade intercepts from the Klondike surface drill program solidified the decision to expand underground development into the Klondike Shoot of the Golden Chest Mine. Concurrent with the decision to expand into the Klondike, Idaho Strategic is also announcing the closing of a modest, oversubscribed private placement to aid in pulling forward the Klondike development schedule and to advance the Company&#8217;s Diamond Creek Rare Earth Element project.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Idaho Strategic has already budgeted and set aside roughly $1,000,000 for its 2022 Diamond Creek Rare Earth Element drill program, which is expected to begin mid-summer. A portion of the funds from this private placement will be used to enhance the original Diamond Creek drill program. The Company also plans to follow up and verify historic sampling and geologic work reported by the Department of Energy (DOE), Unites States Geologic Survey (USGS) and previous owners of the property. Idaho Strategic spent the last year developing the 2022 Diamond Creek drill program based on geologic mapping, sampling and data obtained from numerous historic sources including handwritten journals and conversations with geologists familiar with the property. </P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Funds from the private placement will also be used to expand the underground workings at the Company&#8217;s Golden Chest Mine. &#8220;We are excited about the recent discovery of the Klondike Zone revealed by our Klondike core drilling program because it is close to our existing underground workings and the presence of higher-grade veins within the wider mineralized zone&#8221;, stated Grant Brackebusch, IDR&#8217;s Vice President of Operations. &#8220;For example, a vein intercept in GC 21-207 that assayed 11.8 g/t gold over 1.9 meters is approximately 60 meters from the face of an existing crosscut on the 941 Level. We are making plans to drive a drift from the 941 Level to intercept this vein and to define its dimensions as a future production area.&#8221;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>The Company&#8217;s 2021 underground gold production came solely from the Skookum Shoot area of the mine while drill testing of the Paymaster Shoot to the south of the Skookum, and the Klondike Shoot to the north were underway (Figure 1).  The successful results of the Company&#8217;s </P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>2021 drill program (see January 13th, 2022, press release titled &#8216;Idaho Strategic Drills 16.4 g/t gold over 1.2 m in Paymaster &#8211;&nbsp;Provides Highlights of 2021 Golden Chest Production Expansion Drill Program&#8217;) supports production potential from both the Klondike and Paymaster Shoots. The Company has purchased equipment, hired additional underground development miners and plans to expand underground production from the Skookum Shoot while simultaneously conducting development (to be followed by production later this year) into the Klondike Shoot.</FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>IDR&#8217;s CEO John Swallow adds, &#8220;It is an exciting time for our folks when their hard work pays off and the plan comes together. This is the next step in adding successive production from the Skookum, Klondike, and Paymaster Shoots (see Figure 2). While we have 6+ months of development ahead of us, making this &#8216;production expansion decision&#8217; moves us 2/3<SUP>rds</SUP> of the way toward our goal of 20,000 ounces of annual gold production from the Golden Chest. As seasoned operators we understand there are no guarantees in mining, however the drill results are very impressive, the confidence of our team is palpable, and motivation across the company is high. Once again it is evident that our measured and targeted approach to gold production continues to pay off for our stakeholders.&#8221; </P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>The Company's latest drill results come from the Klondike Shoots&#8217; drillhole GC 21-210. This drillhole was started late in 2021 and completed in January 2022; and marks the second core hole drilled from the second Klondike pad. So far, all the Klondike drill holes have been extraordinary for their sizable (50+ meters) intervals of unbroken lower-grade gold mineralization, enveloping higher-grade gold banded veins. &nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>The intervals below are reported in drill thickness, since vein orientations have yet to be determined, and in grams of gold per tonne (g/t).</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>GC 21-210</FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'> </FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;margin-left:36pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Arial;margin-left:-18pt'>&#9679;</KBD><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>0.74 g/t gold over 51.6 meters (m) from 185.1m to 236.7m including the following higher-grade intervals:</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:36pt'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;margin-left:72pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Arial;margin-left:-18pt'>&#9675;</KBD><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>2.11 g/t gold over 6.1 m from 196.2 to 202.3 m</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;margin-left:72pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Arial;margin-left:-18pt'>&#9675;</KBD><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>1.68 g/t gold over 3.1 m from 209.0 to 212.4 m </FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;margin-left:72pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Arial;margin-left:-18pt'>&#9675;</KBD><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>4.67 g/t gold over1.1 m from 198.9 to 202.3 m </FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;margin-left:36pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Arial;margin-left:-18pt'>&#9679;</KBD><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>14.0 g/t gold over 0.7 m from 249.3 to 250.0 m</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;margin-left:36pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Arial;margin-left:-18pt'>&#9679;</KBD><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>31.7 g/t gold over 0.8 m from 272.2 to 273.0 m</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>GC 21-210 was designed to intercept the same vein package encountered in GC 21-209, only 44 meters down-dip. &nbsp;Much like drillhole GC21-209, GC 21-210 saw the widespread continuous </P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>low-grade gold mineralization, over 51.6 m, with high-grade gold veins as anchors (Figure 2). Some examples of these high-grade gold vein anchors in the Klondike area are: 793 g/t Au over 0.1 m in hole GC 21-208; &nbsp;15.5 g/t Au over 1.0 m in GC21-209; and &nbsp;29.2 g/t Au over 0.8 m also from hole GC 21-209. These widespread areas of gold mineralization show strong silicification and hornfels alteration, which points toward a substantial and deep-rooted mineralizing system. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>IDR's Vice President of Exploration, Rob Morgan commented, &#8220;Many of these thick intercepts of gold mineralization in the Klondike display intense alterations indicative of large-scale deep plumbing, which we believe may lead to new areas of additional gold mineralization. The choice of the Klondike over the Paymaster came down to economics and proximity. We are also looking forward to advancing the Paymaster as those future plans come together.&#8221; </P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>On February&#160;9, 2022, the Company closed subscriptions of US $2,700,000 to its non-brokered private placement (the &#8220;Private Placement&#8221;) with seven investors.&#160;&#160;The Private Placement consisted of shares issued at US $7.50 per common share of restricted stock.&#160; No warrants were issued in connection with the Private Placement.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'><IMG src=nrex99z1_2.jpg width=594 height=349 alt='Picture 1' title='Picture 1'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:14pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:10pt;color:#000000'><B>Figure 1</B></P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=center style='font:16pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'><B><IMG src=nrex99z1_3.jpg width=594 height=416 alt='Picture 2' title='Picture 2'></B>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:14pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:10pt;color:#000000'><B>Figure 2</B></P>

<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Qualified person</FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:10pt;background-color:#FFFFFF'>NJMC's Vice President of Exploration, Robert John Morgan, PG, PLS is a qualified person as such term is defined in National Instrument 43-101 and has reviewed and approved the technical information and data included in this press release.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'><B>About Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc.</B></FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt'>Domiciled in Idaho and headquartered in the Panhandle of northern Idaho, Idaho Strategic Resources (IDR) is one of the few resource-based companies (public or private) possessing the combination of officially recognized U.S. domestic rare earth element properties (in Idaho) and Idaho-based gold production located in an established mining community.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt'>Idaho Strategic Resources produces gold at the Golden Chest Mine located in the Murray Gold Belt (MGB) area of the world-class Coeur d&#8217;Alene Mining District, north of the prolific Silver Valley. With over 7,000 acres of patented and unpatented land, the Company has the largest </P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt'><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>private land position in the area following its consolidation of the Murray Gold Belt for the first time in over 100-years. </FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt'>In addition to gold and gold production, the Company maintains an important strategic presence in the U.S. Critical Minerals sector, specifically focused on the more &#8220;at-risk&#8221; Rare Earth Elements (REE&#8217;s). The Company&#8217;s Diamond Creek and Roberts REE properties are included the U.S. national REE inventory as listed in USGS, IGS and DOE publications. Both projects are located in central Idaho and participating in the USGS Earth MRI program.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>With an impressive mix of experience and dedication, the folks at IDR maintain a long-standing &#8220;We Live Here&#8221; approach to corporate culture, land management, and historic preservation. Furthermore, it is our belief that successful operations begin with the heightened responsibility that only local oversight and a community mindset can provide. Its &#8220;everyone goes home at night&#8221; policy would not be possible without the multi-generational base of local exploration, drilling, mining, milling, and business professionals that reside in and near the communities of the Silver Valley and North Idaho.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>For more information on Idaho Strategic Resources go to <FONT style='color:#1155CC;border-bottom:1px solid #1155CC'>www.idahostrategic.com</FONT> or call: </P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'> &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Monique Hayes, Corporate Secretary/Investor Relations</P>
